  34:     import redis  # noqa: PLC0415 — lazy to defer ImportError to call site
  35:     return redis.Redis.from_url(_redis_url())

  49: def emit_event(
  50:     external_run_id: str | None,
  51:     event_type: str,
  52:     payload: dict[str, Any],
  53:     *,
  54:     redis_client=None,
  55: ) -> None:
  56:     """Best-effort, non-raising XADD to `polaris:events:{run_id}`.
  57: 
  58:     Per Codex iter-1 P1-2: pipeline-A's run_one_query MUST NOT raise
  59:     error_unexpected because Redis is down. All exceptions are caught
  60:     and logged at WARN.

  63:         return
  64:     try:

  66:         client.xadd(
  67:             EVENT_STREAM_KEY.format(run_id=external_run_id),
  68:             {
  69:                 "event_type": event_type,
  70:                 "payload": json.dumps(payload, default=str),
  71:             },
  72:             maxlen=STREAM_MAX_LEN,
  73:             approximate=True,
  74:         )
  75:     except ImportError:
  76:         # redis library not installed (test environment) — silent noop.
  77:         return
  78:     except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 — observability MUST NEVER block pipeline
  79:         # Catch ALL exceptions, not just RedisError, per Codex iter-2 P3 cosmetic.
  80:         logger.warning(

  82:             external_run_id,

  84:             exc,
  85:         )

  88: def emit_terminal_event(

 107: # Translator: pipeline-A event_type → (v6_event_name, transform_fn).
 108: # All terminal pipeline-A events (run.completed/aborted/failed) collapse to v6
 109: # `run_complete` carrying the original status.
 110: _TRANSLATOR: dict[str, tuple[str, Any]] = {
 111:     "scope_gate.completed": ("scope_decision", lambda p: {
 112:         "verdict": p.get("decision", "unknown"),
 113:         "reason": p.get("reason", ""),
 114:     }),
 115:     "corpus_adequacy.completed": ("retrieval_progress", lambda p: {
 116:         "sources_found": p.get("pool_size", 0),

 122:     }),

 124:         "section": p.get("section", ""),

 128:     "generator.section_completed": ("section_complete", lambda p: {

 130:         "verified_sentences": p.get("verified", 0),
 131:         "dropped": p.get("dropped", 0),
 132:     }),
 133:     "run.completed": ("run_complete", lambda p: dict(p)),  # passthrough
 134: }

 136: 
 137: def translate(pipeline_event: dict[str, Any]) -> tuple[str, dict[str, Any]] | None:
 138:     """Translate a pipeline-A event payload to v6 (name, payload) or None."""
 139:     event_type = pipeline_event.get("event_type")
 140:     mapping = _TRANSLATOR.get(event_type or "")
 141:     if mapping is None:
 142:         return None
 143:     v6_name, payload_fn = mapping
 144:     try:
 145:         payload = json.loads(pipeline_event.get("payload", "{}"))
 146:     except json.JSONDecodeError:
 147:         payload = {}
 148:     return v6_name, payload_fn(payload)

 151: # Grace period (seconds) after run_store reports lifecycle_status terminal but
 152: # no Redis terminal event has been seen. After this elapses, emit a synthetic
 153: # `run_complete(status=stream_lost)` so the client gets a deterministic close
 154: # rather than hanging on keepalives forever. Per Codex iter-2 P1-3 + diff iter-1.
 155: STREAM_LOST_GRACE_SECONDS = 10.0
 156:

 158: def _get_lifecycle_status(external_run_id: str) -> str | None:
 159:     """Best-effort sync run_store lookup. Returns lifecycle_status or None.
 160: 
 161:     Imported lazily so tests that don't touch run_store don't pay sqlite init.
 162:     Any failure (missing DB, import error, schema drift) returns None so the
 163:     reader keeps emitting keepalives rather than synthesizing a stream_lost
 164:     terminal on transient backend hiccups.
 165:     """
 166:     try:
 167:         from polaris_v6.queue import run_store  # noqa: PLC0415
 168: 
 169:         row = run_store.get_run(external_run_id)
 170:         if row is None:
 171:             return None
 172:         return getattr(row, "lifecycle_status", None)
 173:     except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 — observability lookup never blocks SSE
 174:         logger.warning(
 175:             "[run_events] run_store lookup failed run_id=%s: %s",
 176:             external_run_id,
 177:             exc,
 178:         )
 179:         return None

 182: async def _check_lifecycle_terminal(external_run_id: str) -> bool:
 183:     """Async wrapper for the sync sqlite lookup."""
 184:     import asyncio  # noqa: PLC0415
 185:     status = await asyncio.to_thread(_get_lifecycle_status, external_run_id)
 186:     # I-rdy-011 (#507): `cancelled` is terminal — a queued-cancel writes no
 187:     # Redis terminal event, so without this an SSE consumer would hang on
 188:     # keepalives until the run is forgotten.
 189:     return status in ("completed", "failed", "cancelled")
 190:

 192: def _is_connection_failure(exc: BaseException) -> bool:
 193:     """Narrow stream_unavailable to actual Redis reachability failures.
 194: 
 195:     Per Codex diff iter-1 P1: every XREAD exception was being mapped to
 196:     stream_unavailable, masking schema bugs / corrupt entries as 'Redis down'.
 197:     Now we treat ONLY connection/timeout/socket failures as unavailability;
 198:     other exceptions surface as stream_lost.
 199:     """
 200:     if isinstance(exc, (ConnectionError, TimeoutError, OSError)):
 201:         return True
 202:     # redis.asyncio raises ConnectionError subclasses; check by class name
 203:     # to avoid a hard import dependency.
 204:     name = type(exc).__name__
 205:     return name in {
 206:         "ConnectionError",
 207:         "TimeoutError",
 208:         "BusyLoadingError",
 209:         "ConnectionResetError",
 210:         "RedisConnectionError",
 211:     }

 214: async def read_events(
 215:     external_run_id: str,
 216:     last_event_id: str = "0-0",
 217:     *,
 218:     block_ms: int = 5000,
 219:     redis_client_async=None,
 220: ) -> AsyncIterator[tuple[str, dict[str, Any]]]:
 221:     """Async generator yielding (stream_id, raw_pipeline_event_dict).
 222: 
 223:     Terminates after emitting a `run.completed` event. Per Codex iter-2 P1-3
 224:     + diff iter-1 P1:
 225: 
 226:     - empty XREAD window → keepalive (caller emits SSE comment frame), then
 227:       check run_store. While lifecycle_status is queued/in_progress, keep
 228:       emitting keepalives.
 229:     - lifecycle_status in {completed, failed} AND no terminal event seen in
 230:       the next STREAM_LOST_GRACE_SECONDS → emit a synthetic
 231:       run_complete(status=stream_lost) and close cleanly.
 232:     - actual Redis connection/timeout failure → emit
 233:       run_complete(status=stream_unavailable) and close.
 234:     - non-reachability XREAD exception → emit stream_lost and close (treat as
 235:       degraded stream rather than 'Redis down').
 236:     """
 237:     import asyncio  # noqa: PLC0415
 238: 
 239:     last_id = _validate_last_event_id(last_event_id)
 240:     key = EVENT_STREAM_KEY.format(run_id=external_run_id)
 241: 
 242:     try:
 243:         if redis_client_async is None:
 244:             import redis.asyncio as aredis  # noqa: PLC0415
 245:             client = aredis.from_url(_redis_url(), decode_responses=False)
 246:         else:
 247:             client = redis_client_async
 248:     except ImportError:
 249:         yield ("0-0", {"event_type": "run.completed", "payload": json.dumps({"status": "stream_unavailable"})})
 250:         return
 251: 
 252:     # Tracks first-seen-at for lifecycle_status terminal so we can apply the
 253:     # grace window before declaring stream_lost.
 254:     lifecycle_terminal_first_seen: float | None = None
 255:     loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()
 256: 
 257:     try:
 258:         while True:
 259:             try:
 260:                 events = await client.xread({key: last_id}, count=100, block=block_ms)
 261:             except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
 262:                 if _is_connection_failure(exc):
 263:                     logger.warning(
 264:                         "[run_events] redis unreachable run_id=%s: %s",
 265:                         external_run_id,
 266:                         exc,
 267:                     )
 268:                     yield ("0-0", {"event_type": "run.completed", "payload": json.dumps({"status": "stream_unavailable"})})
 269:                     return
 270:                 # Non-reachability failure — log and degrade to stream_lost.
 271:                 logger.warning(
 272:                     "[run_events] xread error run_id=%s: %s",
 273:                     external_run_id,
 274:                     exc,
 275:                 )
 276:                 yield ("0-0", {"event_type": "run.completed", "payload": json.dumps({"status": "stream_lost"})})
 277:                 return
 278: 
 279:             if not events:
 280:                 # Empty XREAD window — emit keepalive then consult run_store.
 281:                 yield ("__keepalive__", {})
 282:                 if await _check_lifecycle_terminal(external_run_id):
 283:                     now = loop.time()
 284:                     if lifecycle_terminal_first_seen is None:
 285:                         lifecycle_terminal_first_seen = now
 286:                     elif now - lifecycle_terminal_first_seen >= STREAM_LOST_GRACE_SECONDS:
 287:                         logger.warning(
 288:                             "[run_events] lifecycle terminal without redis terminal "
 289:                             "run_id=%s — emitting synthetic stream_lost",
 290:                             external_run_id,
 291:                         )
 292:                         yield ("0-0", {"event_type": "run.completed", "payload": json.dumps({"status": "stream_lost"})})
 293:                         return
 294:                 else:
 295:                     # Reset the grace window if the run un-terminals (shouldn't happen,
 296:                     # but the lifecycle is the source of truth).
 297:                     lifecycle_terminal_first_seen = None
 298:                 continue
 299: 
 300:             # Real events arrived → reset the grace window.
 301:             lifecycle_terminal_first_seen = None
 302: 
 303:             for _stream_name, entries in events:
 304:                 for entry_id, fields in entries:
 305:                     stream_id = entry_id.decode() if isinstance(entry_id, bytes) else entry_id
 306:                     last_id = stream_id
 307:                     event_type = fields.get(b"event_type") or fields.get("event_type")
 308:                     payload = fields.get(b"payload") or fields.get("payload")
 309:                     if isinstance(event_type, bytes):
 310:                         event_type = event_type.decode()
 311:                     if isinstance(payload, bytes):
 312:                         payload = payload.decode()
 313:                     yield (stream_id, {"event_type": event_type, "payload": payload})
 314:                     if event_type == "run.completed":
 315:                         return
 316:     finally:
 317:         # aredis client lazy-closed via context if possible
 318:         try:
 319:             close = getattr(client, "aclose", None) or getattr(client, "close", None)
 320:             if close:
 321:                 result = close()
 322:                 if hasattr(result, "__await__"):
 323:                     await result
 324:         except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — defensive close
 325:             pass

   1: """Runs router — POST /runs, GET /runs/{id}, POST /runs/{id}/cancel.
   2:

   4: polaris_v6.queue.run_store and enqueue the Dramatiq actor on POST.
   5: Replaces the previous in-memory `_run_table` dict.
   6: 
   7: I-rdy-011 (#507): POST /runs/{id}/cancel — a queued run cancels instantly;
   8: an in-progress run records the cancel request (the worker observes it at
   9: the next pipeline stage boundary). Already-terminal runs are an idempotent
  10: no-op.

  22: from polaris_v6.schemas.run_request import RunRequest
  23: from polaris_v6.schemas.run_status import RunStatusResponse
  24: 
  25: router = APIRouter(prefix="/runs", tags=["runs"])
  26: 
  27: 
  28: @router.post("", response_model=RunStatusResponse, status_code=202)
  29: def create_run(payload: RunRequest) -> RunStatusResponse:

  31:     try:
  32:         run_store.insert_run(run_id, payload.template, payload.question)
  33:     except sqlite3.IntegrityError as exc:
  34:         # uuid4 collision is theoretically impossible but defensive
  35:         raise HTTPException(status_code=409, detail=f"run {run_id!r} already exists") from exc
  36:     except RuntimeError as exc:
  37:         # init_db permission-denied or similar

  42:     record = run_store.get_run(run_id)
  43:     if record is None:  # pragma: no cover — insert just succeeded
  44:         raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="run row vanished after insert")
  45:     return record
  46: 
  47: 
  48: @router.get("/{run_id}", response_model=RunStatusResponse)
  49: def get_run(run_id: str) -> RunStatusResponse:
  50:     record = run_store.get_run(run_id)
  51:     if record is None:
  52:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"run {run_id!r} not found")
  53:     return record
  54: 
  55: 
  56: @router.post("/{run_id}/cancel", response_model=RunStatusResponse)
  57: def cancel_run(run_id: str) -> RunStatusResponse:
  58:     """Request cancellation of a run (I-rdy-011 / #507).
  59: 
  60:     - Unknown run → 404.
  61:     - Already terminal (completed / failed / cancelled) → idempotent no-op,
  62:       returns the current record (200).
  63:     - queued → cancelled instantly; in_progress → cancel requested, the
  64:       worker aborts cooperatively at the next pipeline stage boundary.
  65:     """
  66:     record = run_store.get_run(run_id)
  67:     if record is None:
  68:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"run {run_id!r} not found")
  69:     if record.lifecycle_status in run_store.TERMINAL_STATUSES:
  70:         return record  # idempotent — nothing to cancel
  71: 
  72:     run_store.request_cancel(run_id)
  73: 
  74:     updated = run_store.get_run(run_id)
  75:     if updated is None:  # pragma: no cover — the row existed a line ago
  76:         raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="run row vanished after cancel")

 101: async function asJsonOrThrow<T>(response: Response): Promise<T> {
 102:   const body = await response.json().catch(() => null);
 103:   if (!response.ok) {
 104:     const error = new Error(
 105:       `POLARIS backend returned ${response.status}`,
 106:     ) as ApiError;
 107:     error.status = response.status;
 108:     error.body = body;
 109:     throw error;
 110:   }
 111:   return body as T;
 112: }

   2: 
   3: I-arch-001a (2026-05-12): split lifecycle (operational) from pipeline_status

  10: """
  11: 
  12: from __future__ import annotations
  13: 
  14: from typing import Literal
  15: 
  16: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, computed_field
  17: 
  18: LifecycleStatus = Literal[
  19:     "queued",
  20:     "in_progress",
  21:     "completed",
  22:     "cancelled",
  23:     "failed",
  24: ]
  25:

  33:     "abort_scope_rejected",
  34:     "abort_corpus_inadequate",
  35:     "abort_corpus_approval_denied",
  36:     "abort_no_verified_sections",
  37:     "abort_no_sources",
  38:     "abort_evaluator_critical",
  39:     "error_unexpected",
  40: ]
  41: 
  42: # Backcompat alias used by older code/tests (tests/v6/ asserts body['status']
  43: # and record.status). Computed from lifecycle_status by the model.
  44: RunStatus = LifecycleStatus
  45: 
  46: 
  47: class RunStatusResponse(BaseModel):
  48:     run_id: str = Field(..., description="Server-assigned UUID hex.")
  49:     lifecycle_status: LifecycleStatus = Field(
  50:         ...,
  51:         description="Operational lifecycle: queued → in_progress → completed|failed|cancelled.",
  52:     )
  53:     pipeline_status: PipelineStatus | None = Field(
  54:         default=None,
  55:         description="Pipeline-A manifest verdict. NULL until run reaches a terminal pipeline state.",
  56:     )
  57:     template: str
  58:     question: str
  59:     queued_at: str = Field(..., description="ISO8601 UTC.")
  60:     started_at: str | None = None
  61:     finished_at: str | None = None
  62:     result_json: str | None = None
  63:     error_json: str | None = None

  68:     cost_usd: float | None = None

  70:     # I-rdy-011: True once a cancel has been requested. For a queued run the
  71:     # request is applied atomically (lifecycle_status flips to 'cancelled');
  72:     # for an in_progress run this stays True while lifecycle_status is still
  73:     # 'in_progress', until the worker observes it at a stage boundary.
  74:     cancel_requested: bool = Field(
  75:         default=False,
  76:         description="True iff cancellation has been requested for this run.",
  77:     )
  78: 
  79:     @computed_field  # serialized in JSON and readable as attr

  31: 
  32: export default function RunDetailPage({ params }: RunPageProps) {
  33:   const { runId } = use(params);
  34:   const [status, setStatus] = useState<RunStatusResponse | null>(null);
  35:   const [events, setEvents] = useState<StreamEvent[]>([]);
  36:   const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  37:   const [cancelling, setCancelling] = useState(false);
  38: 
  39:   useEffect(() => {
  40:     let cancelled = false;
  41:     getRun(runId)
  42:       .then((value) => {

  44:       })
  45:       .catch((err) => {
  46:         if (!cancelled) {
  47:           setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Unknown error");
  48:         }
  49:       });

  52:       runId,
  53:       (event) => {

  56:       () => {
  57:         // SSE error: backend may have closed the stream after run_complete.
  58:         source.close();
  59:       },
  60:     );

  63:       cancelled = true;
  64:       source.close();

 255: async def test_read_events_lifecycle_terminal_with_no_redis_event_emits_stream_lost(
 256:     sync_fakeredis, async_fakeredis, monkeypatch
 257: ):
 258:     """Per Codex diff iter-1 P1 (continuing iter-2 brief P1-3): when run_store
 259:     says lifecycle_status='completed' but no Redis terminal event arrives, the
 260:     SSE stream must NOT hang forever on keepalives. After
 261:     STREAM_LOST_GRACE_SECONDS elapses, emit synthetic stream_lost and close.
 262:     """
 263:     # Force the run_store lookup to report 'completed' so empty XREAD windows

 265:     monkeypatch.setattr(
 266:         run_events,
 267:         "_get_lifecycle_status",
 268:         lambda run_id: "completed",
 269:     )
 270:     # Shrink the grace window to keep the test fast.
 271:     monkeypatch.setattr(run_events, "STREAM_LOST_GRACE_SECONDS", 0.05)
 272: 
 273:     seen = []
 274:     async for stream_id, raw in run_events.read_events(
 275:         "rid_grace",
 276:         last_event_id="0-0",
 277:         block_ms=10,
 278:         redis_client_async=async_fakeredis,
 279:     ):
 280:         if stream_id == "__keepalive__":
 281:             seen.append("KEEPALIVE")
 282:             continue
 283:         seen.append(raw["event_type"])
 284:         if raw["event_type"] == "run.completed":
 285:             break
 286:     # Expect: at least one keepalive (first empty window), then synthetic terminal.
 287:     assert seen[-1] == "run.completed"

 296:     ):
 297:         if stream_id == "__keepalive__":
 298:             continue
 299:         payload_seen_last = json.loads(raw["payload"])

 301:     assert payload_seen_last["status"] == "stream_lost"

 305: async def test_read_events_lifecycle_still_running_keepalives_forever(

 307: ):
 308:     """While lifecycle_status is in_progress, empty XREAD windows must keep

  10:  * browser cannot resolve directly). In local dev, INTERNAL_API_URL defaults
  11:  * to http://localhost:8000 so `npm run dev` against a host-port-mapped

  13:  *
  14:  * Codex diff iter-1 P1-B: NEXT_PUBLIC_BACKEND_URL is no longer consulted at

  19: import { authHeader, redirectToSignIn } from "@/lib/auth";
  20: 
  21: const BACKEND_URL = "/api/v6";
  22: 
  23: /**
  24:  * I-rdy-004 (#500) — fetch wrapper for every v6 API call. Injects the
  25:  * `Authorization: Bearer <jwt>` header, preserves any caller-supplied
  26:  * headers, and does NOT force a content-type (so `FormData` uploads keep
  27:  * their auto-generated multipart boundary). On a 401 it clears the token
  28:  * and routes to /sign-in.
  29:  */
  30: async function authFetch(
  31:   url: string,
  32:   init: RequestInit = {},
  33: ): Promise<Response> {
  34:   const headers = new Headers(init.headers ?? {});
  35:   for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(authHeader())) {
  36:     headers.set(key, value);
  37:   }
  38:   const response = await globalThis.fetch(url, { ...init, headers });
  39:   if (response.status === 401) {
  40:     redirectToSignIn();
  41:   }
  42:   return response;
  43: }
  44: 
  45: /**
  46:  * I-rdy-004 — SSE URL for a run's event stream. Native `EventSource` cannot
  47:  * set request headers, so the JWT rides as the `access_token` query param;
  48:  * the backend `require_auth` accepts it for `/stream/*` paths only.
  49:  */
  50: export function streamUrl(runId: string): string {
  51:   const token = authHeader().Authorization?.replace(/^Bearer /, "");
  52:   const base = `${BACKEND_URL}/stream/${encodeURIComponent(runId)}`;
  53:   return token ? `${base}?access_token=${encodeURIComponent(token)}` : base;
  54: }

  30: ) -> AsyncIterator[dict]:

  32: 
  33:     Each yielded event includes `id: <stream_id>` so the EventSource client
  34:     resumes via Last-Event-ID on reconnect. Empty XREAD windows yield a
  35:     keepalive comment frame. Terminates after a v6 `run_complete`.
  36:     """

  38:         run_id,

  41:     ):

  46:         if v6 is None:
  47:             continue
  48:         v6_name, v6_payload = v6
  49:         yield {
  50:             "id": stream_id,
  51:             "event": v6_name,
  52:             "data": json.dumps({"run_id": run_id, **v6_payload}),
  53:         }
  54:         if v6_name == "run_complete":
  55:             return

 362: /**
 363:  * Subscribe to /stream/{runId}. Returns the EventSource so the caller can
 364:  * close it. Per Phase 0 stub, the backend yields 5 deterministic events.
 365:  */
 366: export function subscribeToRun(
 367:   runId: string,
 368:   onEvent: (event: StreamEvent) => void,
 369:   onError?: (error: Event) => void,
 370: ): EventSource {
 371:   const source = new EventSource(streamUrl(runId));
 372: 
 373:   const handler = (event: MessageEvent<string>) => {
 374:     try {
 375:       const parsed = JSON.parse(event.data);
 376:       onEvent({ event: event.type, data: parsed });
 377:     } catch {
 378:       onEvent({ event: event.type, data: { raw: event.data } });
 379:     }
 380:   };
 381: 
 382:   for (const eventName of [
 383:     "scope_decision",
 384:     "retrieval_progress",
 385:     "verifier_verdict",
 386:     "section_complete",
 387:     "run_complete",
 388:   ]) {
 389:     source.addEventListener(eventName, handler);
 390:   }
 391: 
 392:   if (onError) {
 393:     source.onerror = onError;
 394:   }
 395:   return source;
 396: }

+def _abort_if_cancelled(
+    q: dict,
+    run_dir: Path,
+    run_id: str,
+    summary: dict,
+    log_fn,
+) -> bool:
+    """I-rdy-011 (#507): cooperative cancel checkpoint for a v6 run.
+
+    If a cancellation was requested for this v6 run, write a terminal
+    `cancelled` manifest, emit the SSE terminal event, mark the summary, and
+    return True so run_one_query aborts early at this stage boundary. Returns
+    False for non-v6 runs or when no cancel is pending.
+
+    Best-effort: a run_store lookup failure returns False — a healthy run is
+    never aborted on a transient backend hiccup.
+    """
+    ext = q.get("external_run_id")
+    if not (q.get("v6_mode") and ext):
+        return False
+    try:
+        from polaris_v6.queue import run_store
+
+        if not run_store.is_cancel_requested(ext):
+            return False
+    except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — cancel-check failure must not abort a healthy run
+        return False
+    log_fn("[cancel]      cancellation requested — aborting run cooperatively")
+    manifest = {
+        "run_id": run_id,
+        "slug": q.get("slug", ""),
+        "domain": q.get("domain", ""),
+        "question": q.get("question", ""),
+        "status": "cancelled",
+    }
+    (run_dir / "manifest.json").write_text(
+        json.dumps(manifest, indent=2, sort_keys=True) + "\n", encoding="utf-8"
+    )
+    emit_event(ext, "run.completed", {"status": "cancelled"})
+    summary["status"] = "cancelled"
+    return True
+
+

-def mark_in_progress(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> None:

+def mark_in_progress(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> bool:
+    """Transition queued → in_progress IFF the run is not cancel-requested.
+
+    I-rdy-011: compare-and-swap. The `WHERE lifecycle_status='queued' AND
+    cancel_requested=0` guard means a queued cancel that already flipped the
+    row to 'cancelled' cannot be overwritten by a worker picking the run up.
+
+    Returns True iff the row transitioned; False means the run was cancelled
+    (or already past 'queued') and the caller must not run the pipeline.
+    """
+    conn = _connect(path)
+    try:
+        cur = conn.execute(
+            "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='in_progress', started_at=? "
+            "WHERE run_id=? AND lifecycle_status='queued' AND cancel_requested=0",
+            (_now_iso(), run_id),
+        )
+        conn.commit()
+        return cur.rowcount > 0
+    finally:
+        conn.close()
+
+
+def request_cancel(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> str | None:
+    """Request cancellation of a run (I-rdy-011).
+
+    - queued run → atomically transitioned to terminal 'cancelled' (T1,
+      instant — the worker's mark_in_progress CAS will then no-op).
+    - in_progress run → cancel_requested flag set; lifecycle stays
+      'in_progress' until the worker observes the flag at a pipeline stage
+      boundary and calls mark_cancelled (T2, cooperative).
+
+    Returns the resulting lifecycle_status ('cancelled' or 'in_progress'),
+    or None if the run does not exist or is already terminal.
+    """
+    conn = _connect(path)
+    try:
+        # T1: queued → cancelled, atomically.
+        cur = conn.execute(
+            "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='cancelled', cancel_requested=1, "
+            "finished_at=? WHERE run_id=? AND lifecycle_status='queued'",
+            (_now_iso(), run_id),
+        )
+        if cur.rowcount > 0:
+            conn.commit()
+            return "cancelled"
+        # T2: in_progress → set the flag for the worker to observe.
+        cur = conn.execute(
+            "UPDATE runs SET cancel_requested=1 "
+            "WHERE run_id=? AND lifecycle_status='in_progress'",
+            (run_id,),
+        )
+        conn.commit()
+        return "in_progress" if cur.rowcount > 0 else None
+    finally:
+        conn.close()
+
+
+def is_cancel_requested(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> bool:
+    """True iff a cancellation has been requested for the run.
+
+    Best-effort: a missing run / missing table returns False.
+    """
+    conn = _connect(path)
+    try:
+        try:
+            row = conn.execute(
+                "SELECT cancel_requested FROM runs WHERE run_id=?", (run_id,)
+            ).fetchone()
+        except sqlite3.OperationalError:
+            return False
+        return bool(row["cancel_requested"]) if row is not None else False
+    finally:
+        conn.close()
+
+
+def mark_cancelled(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> None:
+    """Terminal transition → lifecycle_status='cancelled' + finished_at.
+
+    Used by the worker when it observes cancel_requested at a pipeline
+    stage boundary (cooperative T2 abort), and as the actor's mapping for a
+    pipeline-A manifest with status 'cancelled'.
+    """
     conn = _connect(path)
     try:
         conn.execute(
-            "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='in_progress', started_at=? WHERE run_id=?",
+            "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='cancelled', cancel_requested=1, "
+            "finished_at=? WHERE run_id=?",
             (_now_iso(), run_id),
         )
         conn.commit()

codex
I found a concrete late-cancel path worth validating: if `cancel_requested` is set after the actor’s startup checks and after the pipeline’s last cancel checkpoint, the actor will still map a successful manifest to `completed`. I’m going to run a small in-process simulation of that exact timing so the verdict is grounded rather than speculative.

import json

from pathlib import Path

root = Path(tempfile.mkdtemp(prefix='codex_i_rdy_011_late_cancel_'))

os.environ['POLARIS_V6_OUTPUT_ROOT'] = str(root / 'v6_runs')

from polaris_v6.queue import run_store
from polaris_v6.queue.actors import enqueue_research_run
import scripts.run_honest_sweep_r3 as sweep

async def fake_run_one_query(q, out_root):
    # Simulate a cancel landing after all actor startup checks and after the
    # pipeline's final cooperative checkpoint, while the final stage is running.
    run_store.request_cancel(q['external_run_id'])
    out_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    manifest = {'run_id': 'SWEEP_late_cancel', 'status': 'success', 'cost_usd': 0.0}
    (out_root / 'manifest.json').write_text(json.dumps(manifest) + '\\n', encoding='utf-8')
    return {'status': 'success', 'manifest': manifest, 'cost_usd': 0.0}
